
# XcAssetConfig

---------
## Calls

---------
### change_existing_asset_location
See [`Pallet::change_existing_asset_location`].
#### Attributes
| Name | Type |
| -------- | -------- | 
| new_asset_location | `Box<VersionedMultiLocation>` | 
| asset_id | `T::AssetId` | 

#### Python

---------
### register_asset_location
See [`Pallet::register_asset_location`].
#### Attributes
| Name | Type |
| -------- | -------- | 
| asset_location | `Box<VersionedMultiLocation>` | 
| asset_id | `T::AssetId` | 

#### Python
```python
call = substrate.compose_call(
```

---------
### remove_asset
See [`Pallet::remove_asset`].
#### Attributes
| Name | Type |
| -------- | -------- | 
| asset_id | `T::AssetId` | 

#### Python
```python
call = substrate.compose_call(
    'XcAssetConfig', 'remove_asset', {'asset_id': 'u128'}
)
```

---------
### remove_payment_asset
See [`Pallet::remove_payment_asset`].
#### Attributes
| Name | Type |
| -------- | -------- | 
| asset_location | `Box<VersionedMultiLocation>` | 

#### Python
```python
call = substrate.compose_call(
    'XcAssetConfig', 'remove_payment_asset', {
    'asset_location': {
```

---------
### set_asset_units_per_second
See [`Pallet::set_asset_units_per_second`].
#### Attributes
| Name | Type |
| -------- | -------- | 
| asset_location | `Box<VersionedMultiLocation>` | 
| units_per_second | `u128` | 

#### Python
```python
call = substrate.compose_call(
    'XcAssetConfig', 'set_asset_units_per_second', {
    'asset_location': {
        None: None,
        'V2': {
            'interior': {
                'Here': None,
                'X1': {
                    'AccountId32': {
                        'id': '[u8; 32]',
                        'network': {
                            'Any': None,
                            'Kusama': None,
                            'Named': 'Bytes',
                            'Polkadot': None,
                        },
                    },
                    'AccountIndex64': {
                        'index': 'u64',
                        'network': {
```

---------
## Events

---------
### AssetLocationChanged
Changed the asset type mapping for a given asset id
#### Attributes
| Name | Type | Composition
| -------- | -------- | -------- |
| previous_asset_location | `VersionedMultiLocation` | ```{None: None, 'V2': {'parents': 'u8', 'interior': {'Here': None, 'X1': {'Parachain': 'u32', 'AccountId32': {'network': 'scale_info::111', 'id': '[u8; 32]'}, 'AccountIndex64': {'network': 'scale_info::111', 'index': 'u64'}, 'AccountKey20': {'network': 'scale_info::111', 'key': '[u8; 20]'}, 'PalletInstance': 'u8', 'GeneralIndex': 'u128', 'GeneralKey': 'Bytes', 'OnlyChild': None, 'Plurality': {'id': 'scale_info::113', 'part': 'scale_info::114'}}, 'X2': ({'Parachain': 'u32', 'AccountId32': 'InnerStruct', 'AccountIndex64': 'InnerStruct', ### UnitsPerSecondChanged
Changed the amount of units we are charging per execution second for an asset
#### Attributes

---------
## Storage functions

---------
### AssetIdToLocation
 Mapping from an asset id to asset type.
 Can be used when receiving transaction specifying an asset directly,
 like transferring an asset from this chain to another.

#### Python
```python
result = substrate.query(
    'XcAssetConfig', 'AssetIdToLocation', ['u128']
)
```

#### Return value

---------
### AssetLocationToId
 Mapping from an asset type to an asset id.
 Can be used when receiving a multilocation XCM message to retrieve
 the corresponding asset in which tokens should me minted.

#### Python
```python
result = substrate.query(
    'XcAssetConfig', 'AssetLocationToId', [
    {
        None: None,
        'V2': {
            'interior': {
                'Here': None,
                'X1': {
                    'AccountId32': {
                        'id': '[u8; 32]',
                        'network': {
                            'Any': None,
                            'Kusama': None,
                            'Named': 'Bytes',
                            'Polkadot': None,
                        },
                    },
                    'AccountIndex64': {
                        'index': 'u64',
                        'network': {
                            'Any': None,
                            'Kusama': None,
                            'Named': 'Bytes',
                            'Polkadot': None,
                        },
                    },
                    'AccountKey20': {
                        'key': '[u8; 20]',
                        'network': {
                            'Any': None,
                            'Kusama': None,
                            'Named': 'Bytes',
                            'Polkadot': None,
                        },
                    },
                    'GeneralIndex': 'u128',
                    'GeneralKey': 'Bytes',
                    'OnlyChild': None,
                    'PalletInstance': 'u8',
                    'Parachain': 'u32',
                    'Plurality': {
                        'id': {
                            'Administration': None,
                            'Defense': None,
                            'Executive': None,
                            'Index': 'u32',
                            'Judicial': None,
                            'Legislative': None,
                            'Named': 'Bytes',
                            'Technical': None,
                            'Treasury': None,
                            'Unit': None,
                        },
                        'part': {
                            'AtLeastProportion': 'InnerStruct',
                            'Fraction': 'InnerStruct',
                            'Members': 'InnerStruct',
                            'MoreThanProportion': 'InnerStruct',
                            'Voice': None,
                        },
                    },
                },
                'X2': (
                    {
```

---------
### AssetLocationUnitsPerSecond
 Stores the units per second for local execution for a AssetLocation.
 This is used to know how to charge for XCM execution in a particular asset.

 Not all asset types are supported for payment. If value exists here, it means it is supported.

#### Python
```python
result = substrate.query(
    'XcAssetConfig', 'AssetLocationUnitsPerSecond', [
    {
        None: None,
        'V2': {
            'interior': {
                'Here': None,
                'X1': {
                    'AccountId32': {
                        'id': '[u8; 32]',
                        'network': {
                            'Any': None,
                            'Kusama': None,
                            'Named': 'Bytes',
                            'Polkadot': None,
                        },
                    },
                    'AccountIndex64': {
                        'index': 'u64',
                        'network': {
                            'Any': None,
                            'Kusama': None,
                            'Named': 'Bytes',
                            'Polkadot': None,
                        },
                    },
                    'AccountKey20': {
                        'key': '[u8; 20]',
                        'network': {
                            'Any': None,
                            'Kusama': None,
                            'Named': 'Bytes',
                            'Polkadot': None,
                        },
                    },
                    'GeneralIndex': 'u128',
                    'GeneralKey': 'Bytes',
                    'OnlyChild': None,
                    'PalletInstance': 'u8',
                    'Parachain': 'u32',
                    'Plurality': {
                        'id': {
                            'Administration': None,
                            'Defense': None,
                            'Executive': None,
                            'Index': 'u32',
                            'Judicial': None,
                            'Legislative': None,
                            'Named': 'Bytes',
                            'Technical': None,
                            'Treasury': None,
                            'Unit': None,
                        },
                        'part': {
                            'AtLeastProportion': 'InnerStruct',
                            'Fraction': 'InnerStruct',
                            'Members': 'InnerStruct',
                            'MoreThanProportion': 'InnerStruct',
                            'Voice': None,
                        },
                    },
                },
                'X2': (
                    {
                        'AccountId32': {
                            'id': '[u8; 32]',
                            'network': 'scale_info::111',
                        },
                        'AccountIndex64': {
                            'index': 'u64',
                            'network': 'scale_info::111',
                        },
                        'AccountKey20': {
                            'key': '[u8; 20]',
                            'network': 'scale_info::111',
                        },
                        'GeneralIndex': 'u128',
```

---------
## Errors

---------
### AssetAlreadyRegistered
Asset is already registered.

---------
### AssetDoesNotExist
Asset does not exist (hasn&\#x27;t been registered).

---------
### MultiLocationNotSupported
Failed to convert to latest versioned MultiLocation
